---

## Prototype Pollution Defenses in `nodejs/node` — Complete Reference

Node.js uses **seven distinct, layered mechanisms** to defend against prototype pollution in its core utilities. Below is the full breakdown by file, symbol, and pattern.

---

### Layer 1 — The Primordials System (`lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js`)

This is the **root of all defenses**. It captures every built-in constructor and method at VM startup, before any user code runs.

| Symbol | What it does |
|---|---|
| `makeSafe(unsafe, safe)` | Creates null-prototype, frozen subclasses of Map/Set/WeakMap/WeakSet. Calls `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(safe.prototype, null)` + `ObjectFreeze(safe.prototype)` |
| `SafeMap`, `SafeSet`, `SafeWeakMap`, `SafeWeakSet` | Null-prototype-frozen collection subclasses — `.get()`/`.set()` cannot be hijacked |
| `hardenRegExp(pattern)` | Overrides all Symbol methods (`Symbol.match`, `Symbol.replace`, `Symbol.split`, etc.) on a RegExp with the original primordial implementations, blocking regex prototype hijacking |
| `SafePromiseAllReturnArrayLike` | Returns `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(returnVal, null)` to prevent pollution on Promise.all results |
| `createSafeIterator` | Iterators with `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(SafeIterator.prototype, null)` + `ObjectFreeze` |
| `copyProps` | Uses `{ __proto__: null, ...desc }` when copying property descriptors |
| `uncurryThis` | Captures `Function.prototype.call` before it can be mutated |

At the very end of the file: `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(primordials, null); ObjectFreeze(primordials)` — the primordials object itself is null-prototype and frozen.

\"deepFreeze\"}\n    67\t  ],\n    68\t  \"text\": \"Node.js defends against prototype pollution in its core utilities through several layered mechanisms, spread across multiple files:\\n\\n## 1. Primordials System (`lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js`)\\nThis is the foundational file. It captures all built-in JavaScript constructors and methods at startup before user code can mutate them. Key defenses:\\n- **`makeSafe(unsafe, safe)`**: Creates safe subclasses of Map, Set, WeakMap, WeakSet, etc. by calling `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(safe.prototype, null)` and `ObjectFreeze(safe.prototype)` \u2014 ensuring the prototype chain cannot be tampered with.\\n- **`SafeMap`, `SafeSet`, `SafeWeakMap`, `SafeWeakSet`**: Null-prototype-frozen subclasses of built-in collections, preventing prototype pollution via `.get()`, `.set()`, etc.\\n- **`hardenRegExp(pattern)`**: Overrides all Symbol methods (`Symbol.match`, `Symbol.replace`, `Symbol.split`, etc.) on a RegExp with the original primordial implementations, preventing user code from hijacking regex operations.\\n- **`SafePromiseAllReturnArrayLike`**: Returns an array-like with `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(returnVal, null)` to avoid prototype pollution on Promise.all results.\\n- **`createSafeIterator`**: Creates iterators with `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(SafeIterator.prototype, null)` and `ObjectFreeze`.\\n- **`copyProps`**: Uses `{ __proto__: null, ...desc }` when copying property descriptors to avoid inheriting from Object.prototype.\\n- **`uncurryThis`**: Captures `Function.prototype.call` before it can be mutated.\\n- At the end: `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(primordials, null); ObjectFreeze(primordials)` \u2014 the primordials object itself is null-prototype and frozen.\\n\\n## 2. Core Utility Helpers (`lib/internal/util.js`)\\n- **`kEmptyObject = ObjectFreeze({ __proto__: null })`**: A frozen null-prototype empty object used as a safe default for options parameters throughout the codebase, preventing `__proto__` injection attacks.\\n- **`kEnumerableProperty = { __proto__: null }`**: A null-prototype property descriptor used with `ObjectDefineProperties` to avoid prototype pollution in property descriptors.\\n- **`filterOwnProperties(source, keys)`**: Uses `{ __proto__: null }` for the result object and `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty(source, key)` to safely filter only own properties, preventing inherited properties from being copied.\\n- **`setOwnProperty(obj, key, value)`**: Uses `ObjectDefineProperty` with a `{ __proto__: null, ... }` descriptor to set properties without going through the prototype chain.\\n- **`SideEffectFreeRegExpPrototypeSymbolReplace` / `SideEffectFreeRegExpPrototypeSymbolSplit`**: Use `getCrossRealmRegex` to create a cross-realm regex that bypasses user-overridden `Symbol.replace`/`Symbol.split` on RegExp.\\n- **`getCrossRealmRegex`**: Creates a regex from a separate realm (via `runInNewContext`) so its prototype methods cannot be polluted by user code.\\n- **`promisify`**: Uses `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(propertiesValues[i], null)` on all property descriptors before passing to `ObjectDefineProperties`, with the comment 'We want to use null-prototype objects to not rely on globally mutable %Object.prototype%'.\\n\\n## 3. ESLint Enforcement (`tools/eslint-rules/avoid-prototype-pollution.js`, `lib/eslint.config_partial.mjs`)\\nA custom ESLint rule (`node-core/avoid-prototype-pollution`) enforces prototype pollution prevention across all lib/ files:\\n- Requires `{ __proto__: null }` in all property descriptors passed to `ObjectDefineProperty`/`ObjectDefineProperties`.\\n- Requires null-prototype objects when returning from async functions.\\n- Bans `RegExpPrototypeTest` (use `RegExpPrototypeExec !== null` instead).\\n- Bans `PromisePrototypeCatch`/`PromisePrototypeFinally` (use safe alternatives).\\n- Bans `ArrayPrototypeConcat` (looks up `@@isConcatSpreadable`).\\n- Requires Proxy handlers to be null-prototype objects.\\n- Flags `ObjectGetOwnPropertyDescriptors` as returning descriptors that inherit from Object.prototype.\\n\\n## 4. HTTP/2 Headers (`lib/internal/http2/compat.js`)\\n- HTTP/2 headers are explicitly initialized using `Object.create(null)` (via `ObjectCreate(null)`) \u2014 the code comments note this is intentional to prevent prototype pollution, unlike HTTP/1 headers which use regular objects for backward compatibility.\\n- `getHeaders()` returns `ObjectAssign({ __proto__: null }, this[kHeaders])` \u2014 a null-prototype copy.\\n\\n## 5. Worker IO (`lib/internal/worker/io.js`)\\n- Uses `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(propertiesValues[i], null)` on all property descriptor values from `ObjectGetOwnPropertyDescriptors(MessagePort.prototype)` before using them, with the explicit comment 'We want to use null-prototype objects to not rely on globally mutable %Object.prototype%'.\\n\\n## 6. Error Serialization (`lib/internal/error_serdes.js`)\\n- `TryGetAllProperties` initializes its accumulator as `{ __proto__: null }` to collect properties without prototype chain interference.\\n\\n## 7. Freeze Intrinsics (`lib/internal/freeze_intrinsics.js`)\\n- Implements deep-freezing of all JavaScript intrinsics when `--frozen-intrinsics` flag is used, preventing any mutation of built-in prototypes.\\n\\n## 8. `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` Pattern\\nUsed pervasively across core modules as a safe replacement for `obj.hasOwnProperty(key)` (which can be overridden). Key files:\\n- `lib/internal/util.js` (filterOwnProperties)\\n- `lib/internal/util/inspect.js`\\n- `lib/internal/async_hooks.js` (getOrSetAsyncId)\\n- `lib/internal/validators.js` (validateThisInternalField)\\n- `lib/internal/errors.js`\\n- `lib/internal/vm/module.js` (isModule)\\n- `lib/internal/cli_table.js`\\n- `lib/internal/crypto/util.js`\\n- `lib/internal/crypto/webidl.js`\\n- `lib/internal/modules/helpers.js`\\n- `lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js`\\n- `lib/internal/source_map/source_map.js`\\n- `lib/internal/tty.js`\\n- `lib/buffer.js`\\n- `lib/cluster.js`\\n- `lib/child_process.js`\\n- `lib/internal/util/inspector.js`\\n\\n## 9. Null-Prototype Objects for Constants/Exports\\n- `lib/quic.js`: Uses `ObjectSeal(ObjectCreate(null, { __proto__: null, ... }))` for all exported constants.\\n- `lib/internal/main/mksnapshot.js`: Uses null-prototype objects for property descriptors.\\n- `lib/internal/per_context/domexception.js`: Uses `{ __proto__: null }` in all `ObjectDefineProperties` calls.\\n- `lib/internal/encoding.js`, `lib/util.js`: Use `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(propertiesValues[i], null)` pattern.\\n\\n## Summary of Key Patterns\\n1. **`Object.create(null)` / `{ __proto__: null }`**: Creates prototype-free objects used as dictionaries, option defaults (`kEmptyObject`), and property descriptors.\\n2. **`ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`**: Safe hasOwnProperty that cannot be overridden by user code.\\n3. **`filterOwnProperties` + `setOwnProperty`**: Safe merge/assign patterns that use null-prototype objects and `ObjectDefineProperty` to avoid prototype chain traversal.\\n4. **`SafeMap`/`SafeSet`/`SafeWeakMap`**: Null-prototype-frozen collection subclasses.\\n5. **`hardenRegExp` + `SideEffectFreeRegExpPrototype*`**: Safe regex operations immune to Symbol method pollution.\\n6. **`kEmptyObject`/`kEnumerableProperty`**: Frozen null-prototype objects for safe defaults and property descriptors.\\n7. **ESLint rule `avoid-prototype-pollution`**: Statically enforces all the above patterns.\"\n    69\t}\n    70\t\n"
